Našim klijentima i jedni drugima. Svakog dana neko započne svoje putovanje sa Transcomom. Uzimajući potencijal koji imaju danas i pretvarajući ga u veštine za budućnost. Dobijanje priznanja za naporan rad, timskog igrača i podršku drugima. Zagovaranje pozitivnih, trajnih promena u svojim timovima i zajednicama. Takvi smo mi u Transcomu. Ovde nam je stalo, i navijamo jedni za druge. Uključeni ste, baš takvi kakvi jeste, od prvog dana. Full range of customer service includes handling of incoming calls and outgoing calls (incl. sales calls). The offered customer service should be of highest quality - accurate, polite, and competent.</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">CSR’s work duties can as well include data input to Clients’ programs and other back office tasks. The BO tasks should be made on the first opportunity, precisely, without mistakes.</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Additional responsibilities may be added as the needs of the business change and expand</span></p></li></ul><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"> </p><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">People</span></p><ul style=\\\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\\\"><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Be open and receptive to constructive feedback from Team Leaders, TQM, and other CSR’s. Listen, ask questions, and enthusiastically implement the tools given to improve the quality of your work.</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Help to keep motivation high by being supportive to your colleagues</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Take full responsibility and the required action for assigned tasks.</span></p></li></ul><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"> </p><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Performance</span></p><ul style=\\\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\\\"><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Understand, meet, and exceed targets set by your TL for different clients/projects.</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Propose motivational activities.</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Propose ideas for continuous improvement.</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Meet or exceed all attendance minimums.</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Adhere to all scheduled breaks and lunches (i.e. meet established schedule adherence/compliance minimums)</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">Zero justified complaints</span></p></li><li dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;\\\"><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; Getting recognized for working hard, being a team player, and supporting others. Championing positive, lasting change in their teams and communities. That’s just how we are at Transcom. Here we care, and root for each other. You’re included, just as you are, from day one. And with the right mindset, there’s no end to how far we can go together.</span></span></p><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"> </p><p dir=\\\"ltr\\\" style=\\\"line-height: 1.38; text-align: justify; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;\\\"><span style=\\\"vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\\\">We are highly driven by our \\\"Malasakit\\\" culture. It means that each one takes part in proactively shaping, cultivating, and building the company we want to work and live in.
